	    function tcfAPIHandler() {
		var gdprApplies;

    <script>
     function sr_menus_setupMainNav_button_inline () {
    if (sr_detect_operaMini || !("classList" in document.createElement("_"))) {
	return false;
    }
    var nav_trigger = document.getElementById('nav_trigger');
    if(!nav_trigger || nav_trigger.triggered) {
	return false;
    }
    nav_trigger.triggered = true;
    var nav = document.getElementById('nav');
    var nav_trigger_a = nav_trigger.querySelector('a');
    if (nav_trigger_a) {
	nav_trigger_a.setAttribute('href','javascript:void(0)');
	nav_trigger.onclick = function (event) {
	    nav.classList.toggle('open');
	    var is_open = nav.classList.contains('open');
	    if (is_open) {
		nav_trigger.classList.add('open');
	    }
	    else {
		nav_trigger.classList.remove('open');
	    }
	    event.preventDefault();
	    try { sr_record_analytics_event('MainNavButtonClick_inline',sr_record_directory(),sr_record_page());}
	    catch(err) {}
	};
    }
    return true;
}
sr_menus_setupMainNav_button_inline();
    </script>

     <div class="" id="stathead_promo">
      <h2>
       <a href="https://stathead.com/?ref=bbr&amp;utm_medium=br&amp;utm_source=bbr_homepage&amp;utm_campaign=basketball">
        Stathead
       </a>
      </h2>
      <div class="adblock">
       <p>
        <a href="https://stathead.com/?ref=bbr&amp;utm_medium=bbr&amp;utm_source=bbr_homepage&amp;utm_campaign=basketball" target="_blank">
         <img alt="Stathead.com Logo" onerror="this.src='https://d2p3bygnnzw9w3.cloudfront.net/req/202004233/logos/stathead-logo.png'; this.onerror = null;" src="https://d2p3bygnnzw9w3.cloudfront.net/req/202004233/logos/stathead-bbr.svg" style="max-width:70%"/>
        </a>
       </p>
       <div>
        <h4>
         The Most Powerful Research Tools in Sports.
        </h4>
        <p>
         Find any player, any team, any season, any game, any play.
        </p>
       </div>
       <p>
        <a class="button stathead_button" href="https://stathead.com/?ref=bbr&amp;utm_medium=bbr&amp;utm_source=bbr_homepage&amp;utm_campaign=basketball" target="_blank">
         <strong>
          Subscribe Now
         </strong>
         (First Month Free)
        </a>
       </p>
      </div>
      <hr/>
      <div>
       <h4>
        Season and Career Finder
       </h4>
       Find single-season or multi-year totals to create leaderboards by team, height, age and more.
       <div class="callout light">
        Ex:
        <a href="https://stathead.com/tiny/lZOnG?&amp;utm_medium=bbr&amp;utm_source=bbr_homepage&amp;utm_campaign=basketball" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
         Which team has the highest average margin of victory in a season?
        </a>
       </div>
       <a href="https://stathead.com/basketball/psl_finder.cgi?&amp;utm_medium=bbr&amp;utm_source=bbr_homepage&amp;utm_campaign=basketball" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
        Player
       </a>
       •
       <a href="https://stathead.com/basketball/tsl_finder.cgi?&amp;utm_medium=bbr&amp;utm_source=bbr_homepage&amp;utm_campaign=basketball" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
        Team
       </a>
      </div>
      <hr/>
      <div>
       <h4>
        Game Finder
       </h4>
       Find individual or groups of games matching a variety of criteria. Includes every game in NBA/BAA regular season and postseason history.
       <div class="callout light">
        Ex:
        <a href="https://stathead.com/tiny/pKWPT?&amp;utm_medium=bbr&amp;utm_source=bbr_homepage&amp;utm_campaign=basketball" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
         What player scored the most points in the first 20 games of their career?
        </a>
       </div>
       <a href="https://stathead.com/basketball/pgl_finder.cgi?&amp;utm_medium=bbr&amp;utm_source=bbr_homepage&amp;utm_campaign=basketball" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
        Player
       </a>
       •
       <a href="https://stathead.com/basketball/tgl_finder.cgi?&amp;utm_medium=bbr&amp;utm_source=bbr_homepage&amp;utm_campaign=basketball" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
        Team
       </a>
      </div>
      <hr/>
      <div>
       <h4>
        <a href="https://stathead.com/basketball/quarter_finder.cgi?&amp;utm_medium=bbr&amp;utm_source=bbr_homepage&amp;utm_campaign=basketball" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
         Player Quarter Finder
        </a>
       </h4>
       Search for the best performances in a quarter by players in the digitized play-by-play era (since 1996-97).
       <div class="callout light">
        Ex:
        <a href="https://stathead.com/tiny/o9BIY?&amp;utm_medium=bbr&amp;utm_source=bbr_homepage&amp;utm_campaign=basketball" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
         Who has the most career postseason 20-point quarters since 1996-97?
        </a>
       </div>
      </div>
      <hr/>
      <div>
       <h4>
        <a href="https://stathead.com/basketball/pspan_finder.cgi?&amp;utm_medium=bbr&amp;utm_source=bbr_homepage&amp;utm_campaign=basketball" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
         Player Span Finder
        </a>
       </h4>
       Find the best/worst spans for any number of seasons, games or days. Find youngest/quickest players to statistical milestones.
       <div class="callout light">
        Ex:
        <a href="https://stathead.com/tiny/loEAL?&amp;utm_medium=bbr&amp;utm_source=bbr_homepage&amp;utm_campaign=basketball" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
         Which players have averaged 30+ PPG over a 5-season span?
        </a>
       </div>
      </div>
      <hr/>
      <div>
       <h4>
        <a href="https://stathead.com/basketball/shot_finder.cgi?&amp;utm_medium=bbr&amp;utm_source=bbr_homepage&amp;utm_campaign=basketball" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
         Player Shot Finder
        </a>
       </h4>
       Run customized searches through every NBA Field Goal Attempt in the digitized play-by-play era (since 1996-97).
       <div class="callout light">
        Ex:
        <a href="https://stathead.com/tiny/ItbV8?&amp;utm_medium=bbr&amp;utm_source=bbr_homepage&amp;utm_campaign=basketball" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
         Who made the most 2-pt jump shots in a season since 1996-97?
        </a>
       </div>
      </div>
      <hr/>
      <div>
       <h4>
        <a href="https://stathead.com/basketball/h2h_finder.cgi?&amp;utm_medium=bbr&amp;utm_source=bbr_homepage&amp;utm_campaign=basketball" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
         Head2Head Finder
        </a>
       </h4>
       Find out how any 2 players in NBA history have fared against each other head-to-head. Includes team records and individual statistics.
       <div class="callout light">
        Ex:
        <a href="https://stathead.com/tiny/kgbxx?&amp;utm_medium=bbr&amp;utm_source=bbr_homepage&amp;utm_campaign=basketball" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
         Magic Johnson vs Larry Bird
        </a>
       </div>
      </div>
     </div>
